<rating>5</rating><text>I write for a music and coffee blog called Crooners In Coffeeshops, in which I interview local musicians at local coffeeshops. My writeup reflects the positive experience that I encountered at Caffe Luxxe on our interview date.

L.A. based small batch coffee roaster Caffe Luxxe is wonderful example of what can grow from the powerful bond of friendship, specifically one that spans decades like that of owners Mark Wain and Gary Chau. Taking the chance to quit their corporate jobs in 2006, they‚Äôve been able to fuel their business from their personal relationship and their love for European luxury caffe culture.

A fun fact, Caffe Luxxe is the first of its kind in L.A. for artisan coffee preparation, and boy golly, it is not one to miss at any of its So Cal locations. The coffee world is your oyster when picking your beverage of choice from their delectable menu of drips, pour overs, and a unique variety of Bevande Di Caffe (including a chocolate-y shaken Caffe Shakerato, a sparkling espresso Caffe Frizzante, and a spiced citrus Caffe Nico). If seasonal specials are your thing, have no fear, because they‚Äôve got those covered too! What more could you ask for?</text>< pics>

< Text>
Pretty chill cafe tucked into a strip mall. I felt like it was a bit difficult to see from the street in light traffic but some of that is due to the rarity with which I am on that side of town. The employees were friendly and knowledgeable while the cafe itself was immaculately clean, well-laid out and inviting. The reason for my visit was specifically the espresso beans I had read about recently. They did not disappoint in the least, and pull a great shot after very little tweaking of my grinder. Any single point I listed would be enough to keep Caffe Luxxe in the rotation; the synergy of them all makes the drive somewhat more enjoyable.<//Text>

Quality is top notch. At so many donut shops you get a bunch of different shaped donuts but they all taste the same. Old Fashioned Donuts is not like the rest. Cherry frosting taste like cherry, maple frosting a like maple, you get the idea. One of the best buttermilk and old fashioned around. But the true standout for me is the rainbow sprinkles donut holes. No matter what you order, don‚Äôt walk out with at least a couple dozen of these colorful little nuggets of flavor! Perfectly fried cake and the frosting and sprinkles layer is almost crunchy. They don‚Äôt skimp on the sprinkles either.<//review>

<rate>4<//rate>< text>
I forget what business they replaced, but I think coffee shop. Bright place with boba industry setting. Seating is limited to a communal like table, but a few tables outside as well. The employees are cool, witty and outspoken. Took me about three minutes to decide what I want, but that's when they come through. Told them why I like and don't like, then they made suggestion. Drink is alright made to my specifications of no ice and low sugar. Boba were nice and chewy not to soft and holds shape of roundness. They were up front when asked if it was real taro pieces or powder. It was the latter, but at least I know ahead of time.<//text>

I've tried their "Matcha Blossom" (which is essentially a matcha latte with strawberry puree) and I thought it was just ok.  It would have been nice if they had milk alternatives, which they didn't.  I haven't tried any of their other drinks, but I definitely would not go out of my way to come here.  This is a nice place to stop by for boba only if you are in the neighborhood.  Whats nice about this place is that they have some games for you to play if you're hanging out.</text>

Elk Grove Pediatrics is NOT the same quality doctors office it once was. The support staff has completely changed. After a rather large mix-up in regards to a vaccine given to my daughter in October, and confusion as to which one was due because her record showed she had been given flu shot, which she happens to be allergic to, I have less than favorable opinion in regards to not only their organizational skills, but mostly their LACK of professionalism.  When nurse assistant called to let me know the mix up was straightened out and not to worry, I asked that her supervisor called and requested the documentation to reflect the corrected mistake. I was told no I could not have a copy of paperwork, and no one, not nurse or more importantly the doctor whom my daughter has seen since she was 5, qnow 14, didn't even have the kindness to call me to apologize or reassure me this mistake was simply a clerical error. I had truly thought she was a good doctor, who really had me fooled, as I thought lal these years she cared. Clearly the office has a total lack of organization, as well as complete lack of professionalism. You don't tell me my daughter is due for her 2nd HPV vaccine, when she supposedly had it 6 months prior. And then tell me she had the flu shot instead.!?! This office is not a good doctors office for children, and families.
I only gave star so it allowed me to post.
I think people should know. Patients and families deserve better!<//Text>

I've brought in simple paperwork to my son's appointments before and they refuse to sign it at the time of the appointment even though it literally takes 2 seconds, they say it will be processed within 3 business days. They charge $$ for immunization cards. My son needed special formula and I've spoken to his doctor at an appointment about getting the prescription so insurance can cover it. For 6 weeks they didn't submit a prescription to the pharmacy even after the pharmacy called AND faxed them nearly everyday. They claimed to have sent it and finally returned my call 6 weeks later to blame the pharmacy for "possibly losing it." Within the 6 weeks of waiting for the prescripthion, I've had multiple people from the office give me FALSE information such as "oh we don't write prescriptions for special formula" etc. For my son's 12 mo, they had us go to quest for blood work. Other offices do it at the office and it's a simple poke in the finger. Overall this office has been a headache!!! I've finally been able to switch to another one. Don't waste your time here.</Review>

< Text>
I bring my daughter in every month or so for her wellness checks and the doctors and staff are always friendly and courteous. It's usually a minimal wait time and you're in and out pretty fast with a summary of the visit.
The only complaint I have is that in the waiting room there are two TVs that are constantly on and I got into an argument with the receptionists when I asked them to turn them off. My daughter is only 7 months old and I don't want her watching TV. The American Academy of Pediatrics strongly recommends no TV until after two years old because it can damage their brains at such a young age and inhibit proper development. And even after two it's only supposed to be 15 minutes a day with parent interaction. The doctors also advise at this clinic (Elk Grove pediatrics) to limit screen time. So the fact that there two TVs constantly on in the waiting room that are filled with children is completely bizarre to me. I'm going to turn the TV off everytime I go there and if becomes an issue I'll find another clinic where the receptionists are not addicted to TV and our children are not being zombified.< /Text>
